Received response: int getint(int *pn) {
    int c, sign;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) // skip white space
        ;

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-') {
        ungetch(c); // it is not a number
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
        if (!isdigit(c)) {
            ungetch(sign == 1 ? '+' : '-');
            return 0;
        }
    }

    for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        *pn = 10 * *pn + (c - '0');

    *pn *= sign;

    if (c != EOF)
        ungetch(c);

    return c;
}

Received response: {
  char c;
  while ((c = getch()) == ' ' || c == '\t')
    ;
  if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-')
  {
    ungetch(c);
    return 0;
  }
  int sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
  if (c == '+' || c == '-')
  {
    c = getch();
    if (!isdigit(c))
    {
      ungetch(sign == 1 ? '+' : '-');
      return 0;
    }
  }
  for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
    *pn = *pn * 10 + (c - '0');
  *pn *= sign;
  if (c != EOF)
    ungetch(c);
  return c;
}

char *gettoken() {
    int c;
    char *token = &buf[bufp];
    
    while((c = getchar()) != EOF && !isspace(c)) {
        *token++ = c;
    }
    
    *token = '\0';
    
    return &buf[bufp];
}

```c
int getch(void) {
    int ch;

    // Read the next character from the standard input
    ch = getchar();

    // If the character is not the end of file
    if (ch != EOF) {
        // If the character is not a newline
        if (ch != '\n') {
            // Read characters until newline or end of file is reached
            while ((ch = getchar()) != '\n' && ch != EOF) {
                continue;
            }
        }
        // If the character is a newline, ignore it and return the newline character
        return '\n';
    } else {
        // Return end of file character
        return EOF;
    }
}
```

                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 3.0374491214752197 seconds
Received response: int getint()
{
  int c, sign, value;
  
  while (isspace(c = getch())) {} // skip white space
  
  if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-')
  {
    ungetch(c);
    return 0; // not a number
  }
  
  sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
  if (c == '+' || c == '-')
  {
    c = getch();
    if (!isdigit(c))
    {
      ungetch(sign == 1 ? '+' : '-');
      return 0; // not a number
    }
  }
  
  for (value = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
  {
    value = 10 * value + (c - '0');
  }
  
  value *= sign;
  
  if (c != EOF)
  {
    ungetch(c);
  }
  
  return value;
}

                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 2.266334056854248 seconds
Received response: int getint(int *pn)
{
    int c, sign;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) // skip white space
        ;
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-')
    {
        ungetch(c); // not a number
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-')
    {
        c = getch();
        if (!isdigit(c))
        {
            ungetch((sign == 1) ? '+' : '-');
            return 0;
        }
    }
    
    for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        *pn = 10 * *pn + (c - '0');
    
    *pn *= sign;
    
    if (c != EOF)
        ungetch(c);
    
    return c;
}

                'next token or line'
                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 2.311436414718628 seconds
Received response: int getint()
{
   // next token or line
   char c;
   int sign, value;

   while(isspace(c = getch())) // skip white space
      ;

   if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-')
   {
      ungetch(c); // it is not a number
      return 0;
   }

   sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

   if (c == '+' || c == '-')
   {
      c = getch();
      if (!isdigit(c))
      {
         ungetch(sign == -1 ? '-' : '+'); // there is not a number after the sign
         return 0;
      }
   }

   for (value = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
   {
      value = 10 * value + (c - '0');
   }

   value *= sign;

   if (c != EOF)
   {
      ungetch(c); // put back the non-digit character
   }

   return value;
}

    return c;
}

  sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

  // Skip '+' or '-' character
  if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
    c = getchar();
  }

  // Process digits
  for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getchar()) {
    *pn = 10 * *pn + (c - '0');
  }

  *pn *= sign;

    ungetc(c, stdin);
  }

  return c;
}
